<a id="1823" class="Keyword">private</a> <a id="1831" class="Keyword">variable</a>  <a id="1841" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1841" class="Generalizable">Î±</a> <a id="1843" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1843" class="Generalizable">Ïáµƒ</a> <a id="1846" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1846" class="Generalizable">Î²</a> <a id="1848" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1848" class="Generalizable">Ïáµ‡</a> <a id="1851" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1851" class="Generalizable">Î³</a> <a id="1853" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1853" class="Generalizable">Ïá¶œ</a> <a id="1856" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1856" class="Generalizable">Î¹</a> <a id="1858" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1860" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a>

Recall, `f ~ g` means f and g are *extensionally* (or pointwise) equal; i.e., `âˆ€ x, f x â‰¡ g x`. We use this notion of equality of functions in the following definition of *isomorphism*.

We could define this using Sigma types, like this.

```agda
_â‰…_ : {Î± Î² : Level}(ğ‘¨ : Algebra Î± ğ‘†)(ğ‘© : Algebra Î² Ïáµ‡) â†’ Type(ğ“ âŠ” ğ“¥ âŠ” Î± âŠ” Î²)
ğ‘¨ â‰… ğ‘© =  Î£[ f âˆˆ (hom ğ‘¨ ğ‘©)] Î£[ g âˆˆ hom ğ‘© ğ‘¨ ] ((âˆ£ f âˆ£ âˆ˜ âˆ£ g âˆ£ â‰ˆ âˆ£ ğ’¾ğ’¹ ğ‘© âˆ£) Ã— (âˆ£ g âˆ£ âˆ˜ âˆ£ f âˆ£ â‰ˆ âˆ£ ğ’¾ğ’¹ ğ‘¨ âˆ£))
```

However, with four components, an equivalent record type is easier to work with.

   <a id="3374" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="3383" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3383" class="Function">Î¾</a> <a id="3385" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3387" href="Overture.Basic.html#4303" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3389" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2702" class="Field">to</a> <a id="3392" href="Overture.Basic.html#4303" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3394" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1783" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="3398" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3399" href="Overture.Basic.html#4303" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3401" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2718" class="Field">from</a> <a id="3406" href="Overture.Basic.html#4303" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3408" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1783" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="3412" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3354" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3413" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3415" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2580" class="Function Operator">â‰ˆâ‚‚</a> <a id="3418" href="Overture.Basic.html#4303" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3420" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2702" class="Field">to</a> <a id="3423" href="Overture.Basic.html#4303" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3425" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1783" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="3429" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3430" href="Overture.Basic.html#4303" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3432" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2718" class="Field">from</a> <a id="3437" href="Overture.Basic.html#4303" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3439" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1783" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="3443" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3358" class="Bound">y</a><a id="3444" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="3449" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3383" class="Function">Î¾</a> <a id="3451" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3453" href="Function.Bundles.html#1938" class="Field">cong</a> <a id="3458" href="Overture.Basic.html#4303" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3460" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2702" class="Field">to</a> <a id="3463" href="Overture.Basic.html#4303" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3465" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3361" class="Bound">xy</a>
   <a id="3471" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3471" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="3476" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3478" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3354" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3480" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2580" class="Function Operator">â‰ˆâ‚‚</a> <a id="3483" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3358" class="Bound">y</a>
   <a id="3488" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3471" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="3493" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3495" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2610" class="Function">transâ‚‚</a> <a id="3502" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3503" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2594" class="Function">symâ‚‚</a> <a id="3508" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3509" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2736" class="Field">toâˆ¼from</a> <a id="3517" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3354" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3518" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3521" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3522" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2610" class="Function">transâ‚‚</a> <a id="3529" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3383" class="Function">Î¾</a> <a id="3531" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3532" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2736" class="Field">toâˆ¼from</a> <a id="3540" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3358" class="Bound">y</a><a id="3541" class="Symbol">))</a>

</pre>

That is, two structures are *isomorphic* provided there are homomorphisms going back and forth between them which compose to the identity map.


#### <a id="properties-of-isomorphisms-of-setoid-algebras">Properties of isomorphism of setoid algebras</a>

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3825" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="3830" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2627" class="Module Operator">_â‰…_</a>

<a id="3868" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3835" class="Function">â‰…-refl</a> <a id="3875" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3876" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3876" class="Bound">Î±</a><a id="3877" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3879" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3879" class="Bound">Ïáµƒ</a><a id="3881" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3883" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3883" class="Bound">ğ‘¨</a><a id="3884" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3886" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3888" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2685" class="InductiveConstructor">mkiso</a> <a id="3894" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Properties.html#3541" class="Function">ğ’¾ğ’¹</a> <a id="3897" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Properties.html#3541" class="Function">ğ’¾ğ’¹</a> <a id="3900" class="Symbol">(Î»</a> <a id="3903" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3903" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="3905" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="3907" href="Relation.Binary.Structures.html#1568" class="Function">refl</a><a id="3911" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3913" class="Symbol">Î»</a> <a id="3915" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3915" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="3917" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="3919" href="Relation.Binary.Structures.html#1568" class="Function">refl</a>

  <a id="4954" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4954" class="Function">lem1</a> <a id="4959" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4961" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4924" class="Bound">aâ‚€</a> <a id="4964" href="Relation.Binary.Bundles.html#1098" class="Function Operator">â‰ˆ</a> <a id="4966" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4967" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4910" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="4969" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1783" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="4973" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4974" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4902" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="4976" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1783" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="4980" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4924" class="Bound">aâ‚€</a><a id="4982" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="5058" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5009" class="Function">lem2</a> <a id="5063" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5065" href="Function.Bundles.html#1938" class="Field">cong</a> <a id="5070" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4910" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="5072" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4932" class="Bound">fafb</a>

  <a id="5128" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5128" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="5133" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5135" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4924" class="Bound">aâ‚€</a> <a id="5138" href="Relation.Binary.Bundles.html#1098" class="Function Operator">â‰ˆ</a> <a id="5140" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4928" class="Bound">aâ‚</a>
  <a id="5145" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5128" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="5150" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5152" href="Relation.Binary.Structures.html#1620" class="Function">trans</a> <a id="5158" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4954" class="Function">lem1</a> <a id="5163" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5164" href="Relation.Binary.Structures.html#1620" class="Function">trans</a> <a id="5170" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5009" class="Function">lem2</a> <a id="5175" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5079" class="Function">lem3</a><a id="5179" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="5183" class="Comment">-- The &quot;from&quot; map of an isomorphism is injective.</a>
<a id="â‰…fromInjective"></a><a id="5233" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5233" class="Function">â‰…fromInjective</a> <a id="5248" class="Symbol">:</a>  <a id="5251" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5252" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5252" class="Bound">ğ‘¨</a> <a id="5254" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5256" href="Setoid.Algebras.Basic.html#2865" class="Record">Algebra</a> <a id="5264" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1841" class="Generalizable">Î±</a> <a id="5266" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1843" class="Generalizable">Ïáµƒ</a><a id="5268" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5270" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5270" class="Bound">ğ‘©</a> <a id="5272" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5274" href="Setoid.Algebras.Basic.html#2865" class="Record">Algebra</a> <a id="5282" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1846" class="Generalizable">Î²</a> <a id="5284" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1848" class="Generalizable">Ïáµ‡</a><a id="5286" class="Symbol">}</a>
                  <a id="5306" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5307" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5307" class="Bound">Ï†</a> <a id="5309" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5311" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5252" class="Bound">ğ‘¨</a> <a id="5313" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2627" class="Record Operator">â‰…</a> <a id="5315" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5270" class="Bound">ğ‘©</a><a id="5316" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5318" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="5320" href="Setoid.Functions.Injective.html#2164" class="Function">IsInjective</a> <a id="5332" href="Overture.Basic.html#4303" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="5334" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2718" class="Field">from</a> <a id="5339" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5307" class="Bound">Ï†</a> <a id="5341" href="Overture.Basic.html#4303" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a>

<a id="5344" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5233" class="Function">â‰…fromInjective</a> <a id="5359" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5359" class="Bound">Ï†</a> <a id="5361" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5363" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4830" class="Function">â‰…toInjective</a> <a id="5376" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5377" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3970" class="Function">â‰…-sym</a> <a id="5383" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5359" class="Bound">Ï†</a><a id="5384" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

Fortunately, the lift operation preserves isomorphism (i.e., it's an *algebraic invariant*). As our focus is universal algebra, this is important and is what makes the lift operation a workable solution to the technical problems that arise from the noncumulativity of Agda's universe hierarchy.

           <a id="6663" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6664" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6272" class="Function">Lift-Alg-isoÊ³</a> <a id="6678" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5755" class="Function">Lift-â‰…Ë¡</a><a id="6685" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

The lift is also associative, up to isomorphism at least.

</pre>

Products of isomorphic families of algebras are themselves isomorphic. The proof looks a bit technical, but it is as straightforward as it ought to be.

<pre class="Agda">

   <a id="8629" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8629" class="Function">Ïˆâˆ¼Ï•</a> <a id="8633" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8635" class="Symbol">âˆ€</a> <a id="8637" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8637" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8639" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="8641" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8642" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8307" class="Function">Ïˆ</a> <a id="8644" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1783" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="8648" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8649" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8068" class="Function">Ï•</a> <a id="8651" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1783" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="8655" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8637" class="Bound">a</a><a id="8656" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="8659" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7840" class="Function Operator">â‰ˆâ‚</a> <a id="8662" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8637" class="Bound">a</a>
   <a id="8667" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8629" class="Function">Ïˆâˆ¼Ï•</a> <a id="8671" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8671" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8673" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8675" class="Symbol">Î»</a> <a id="8677" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8677" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="8679" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="8681" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2790" class="Field">fromâˆ¼to</a> <a id="8689" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8690" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8016" class="Bound">AB</a> <a id="8693" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8677" class="Bound">i</a><a id="8694" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8696" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8671" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8698" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8677" class="Bound">i</a><a id="8699" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

A nearly identical proof goes through for isomorphisms of lifted products.

<pre class="Agda">
